***prent.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:prent.html>prent</a> (23046)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">prente</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>This</a> etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:incomplete.html>incomplete</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:you.html>You</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:can.html>can</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:help.html>help</a> Wiktionary <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> elaborating <a href = vnd.unilang:on.html>on</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> origins <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>this</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:term.html>term</a>.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prent.html>prent</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prenten.html>prenten</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prentje.html>prentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***preuts.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:preuts.html>preuts</a> (14317)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">preus</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">prues</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">pruets</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">preux</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">proz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prōdest</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:useful.html>useful</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:preuts.html>preuts</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:preuts.html>preutser</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meest.html>meest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:preuts.html>preuts</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">preutst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:prudish.html>prudish</a></span>, exaggeratedly <a href = vnd.unilang:proper.html>proper</a>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:modest.html>modest</a></span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:priapisme.html>priapisme</a> (73440)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πριαπισμός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priapismós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:priapisme.html>priapisme</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:priapisme.html>priapismen</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">priapismes</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:priem.html>priem</a> (44823)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:priem.html>priem</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*preumaz</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Preem</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Pfriem</i>), alteration <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*preunaz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*brewn-</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">briaunà</i> ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:edge.html>edge</a>’, Albanian <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">brez</i> ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:belt.html>belt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:girdle.html>girdle</a>’).

***prijzen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:prijzen.html>prijzen</a> (3905)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">prisen</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">priser</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pretiō</i>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">primaet</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">primat</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prīmātus</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prīmus</i>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:religion.html>religion</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> primate, high-ranking <a href = vnd.unilang:clergyman.html>clergyman</a>
